< review>
Stayed on Venice beach for a 2 day stay and wanted some late night eats. Made it a half hour before close and they were so nice in still accommodating us. Ordered their Combination Fried Rice. Absolutely amazing presentation and some of the best fried rice ive ever had. My mate had their curry and only had good things to say. Highly recommend this place if your visiting or living nearby looking for good food.< /review>

< Text>
Food is delicious. 5 stars. But...

Minus one star because I've only got a 50% success rate of getting "very spicy" when I order. Tonight I specified max spicy, saw "2 stars" on the receipt when I picked up my order, then got home to find no chili in my dish whatsoever. I got more of a burn from my piping hot soup than I did from my main dish.

Please. When I say "extra spicy" I MEAN IT. Don't give me Midwestern White Guy spicy. It's enough to make me stop ordering.<//Text>

<Review>This place used to be my favorite Thai spot, but they renovated during the pandemic and added a new seating area and it appears that they cannot keep up with the increase of dine in customers.  I have ordered from here 3 times in the past month and every time it takes at least twice as long as the wait time they give you.  The first time I went back it took an hour and 20 minutes for egg rolls and a noodle dish (they were packed I will give them that) the second time I went back I gave them an extra 10 min until I drove over to get my food and they forgot to put in my order they said it will be ready in 10 minutes, I come back and they forgot to put in my order the second time as well, making me wait around an hour and a half again, for egg rolls and a noodle dish, this last time I went they gave me a 30 minutes wait time, I came 30 min late anticipating the super long wait, and still had to wait another 30 min in the restaurant so it took them an another hour and a half to make my food and they skimped me on an egg rolls on top of all of that, once again this place used to be my favorite Thai place, but because of these experiences I‚Äôve had since the remodel I cannot say that I will be returning even though the food is amazing I cannot deal with the wait times being 3X longer than they tell me and skimping me on top of all of it.  Hope you guys can get it together at some point.< /Review></record>

< Text>
Excellent service and quality!

The menu was clean and organized. Finally a menu with lots of nice pictures of foods. Excellent and so helpfulI. I wish other restaurant's menu could have more pictures.

The staff were kind and helpful.

As we entered in to the restaurant during lunch time, many visitors were there to eat.

We were quickly helped to sit down at a table and right away and another waitress came to receive our order.

We ordered several different dishes. The food were hot, fresh and tasted excellent!

The amount of salt in the food was ok but the amount of sugar in salads and other dishes were more than expected. We wish the sugar could be less and they could serve some sugar at side so the customer themself can decide how much sugar they want to add.

The waiting time from order to be served was ok.

The restroom:
We didn't see any restroom. Does this place have restroom?

Here are some pictures I took.</Text>

< name>
Dave Dudley</name>
<Time>1583850607843< /Time><rating>5</rating>< text>
What a wonderful place.  We stopped here after touring the Venice Canal houses.  We had the Krispy Ka Prao Chicken and the Roasted Duck Curry with a side of white, steamed rice.

First, the ambiance is just amazing. We sat outside, our table overlooking the canal, a fresh breeze lightly blowing in on a warm and sunny winter day.

The chicken was tender, falling off the bone, with a sticky, crispy skin and crispy basil. I probably could have eaten another entire serving.  The curry had a beautiful kick of spice to it and the duck was tasty.

The service was great too.  The server kept our water glasses full and checked in on us several times.

We would definitely return here again.<//text>

< Review>
Superb, authentic Thai food. We cook and travel internationally a lot and are choosy about where we eat, but this restaurant was so good we ate here two days in a row.

For salads, we loved the glass noodle salad as well as the papaya salad (Som Tum). The Siamese Hot Pot Delight soup is delicious and lovely. The Deep Sea Diamond from the specialty menu was also great. Even the mango sticky rice had a special touch. Oh, and their fresh coconuts are delicious! Very fresh.

The patio is lovely in good weather and they have kind service.< /Review>

< text>
The first I came, i wasn‚Äôt too impressed with my food. The staff were friendly and explained their menu, the restaurant was clean, and the food was fresh. I wanted to give it a second try since it‚Äôs so close to my work and something told me to go back. My second visit definitely redeemed this place! I joined the rewards program and will most likely be returning on my lunch breaks.

First try: French Quarter Grain bowl
-rice very bland
-red onions very overwhelming
-for $11 I thought it would be a lot bigger and planned to keep it for leftovers. It was a lot smaller than expected, but I still finished and felt full.

Second try: On the Border Green Bowl
-lots of flavor
-this bowl seemed bigger than the grain bowl, and I ended up saving half for later. Same price as the grain bowl.

They offer bowls (create your own in available), breakfast, smoothies, juices, soups, and a kids menu (they even have a little kids table which is so cute). Indoor and outdoor seating available. A grab & go refrigerator is loaded with water, juices, snacks, and fruit. Definitely recommend!!<//text>

<Date>1615783414037<//Date>< text>
Picked up a pair of ski boots there today. Staff were super nice and knowledgeable. They were very patient and detailed explaining the ins and outs of the boots. They found the best fitting pair for my feet and my special situations. I am an advanced snowboarder but beginner skier. So its best for me to go with slightly high flex, but not too high since I am not a big person. They taught me the proper way to put the boots on and how to maximize the life of them. This kind of expert advices don't exist on Amazon. In fact, for the few pairs of boots I looked at, REI's prices  are super competitive even to the internet only sellers.

The store is huge with lots of other outdoor treasures. They also sell bikes and do repairs. Tons of camping stuff.

Worth noting that their website is awesome. It's easy to browse stuff on their website, then find out if the item is in stock in the local store. Then just go there to check out the real thing and walk out with it!< /text>

<review>I would like to preface with saying that I am a long time REI member and have never had a bad experience in any of their other stores. That being said, I have to give a bad review here for bad customer service and staff that were not knowledgeable.

Long story short is that they sold my fiance ski boots that wouldn't work with her skis/bindings(we even brought the skis into the store when buying boots to avoid this). We left them there for them to be tuned for safety. We got a call back saying that they weren't compatible. When we picked them up they more or less shrugged and wrote down a part number for new outsoles that we needed to source ourselves in order to make the boots work with the bindings. Not great customer service.

We did end up ordering the part directly from the manufacturer, but guess what? They were not compatible because they were 5355 outsoles, and the boots are compatible with 9523 outsoles. I figured this out after getting fed up with all the terrible advice we have been getting and went online to figure it all out for myself.

In the end, we needed to return the boots, beg for a refund from k2 for the outsoles, and find another shop to buy boots at. Props to REI for such a good return policy. That's the only reason the review is 2 stars.

We wasted a lot of time and money. The whole reason I go to a store like this is for the expert advice and to save time so I don't have to learn everything myself about ski boots and bindings compatibility. Because of the lack of knowledge and poor service I ended up learning a lot about ski boots and bindings, but I'm busy and my time means a lot to me. I hate wasting it.</review>< Pics>

<Review>I came here to buy some hiking boots for a trek. Looking confused in the shoe section, I was quickly approached by a staff member who asked me a bunch of questions about my trek and specifics about my feet. He took measurements and we seriously went through about 10 different pairs of shoes to narrow down which brand and fit worked best. Each round of shoes got better and better until we found the absolute perfect Vasque boots. Yes, REI is overpriced, especially when it comes to shoes. But honestly I'm completely OK paying extra for the service. They worked to find me the right shoe, not to up-sell me to something to make higher commission, like other stores. I've since become a member and am coming back here for all my outdoors needs!</Review>< Name>

<Rating>5< /Rating><text>I love this sexy wine bar!  My girlfriends and I met for lunch right when they opened today.  We chose to sit on their couches instead of the wine barrel tables.  I wanted to relax and put my feet up.  They also have seating outside for you sun goddesses.

We decided to order a little of everything.  They're small plates (2-4 items).  We had the juicy mouth watering soft tacos.  Those by far were my favorite!  We also ordered the garlic bread.  It had a special mixture of mayo and parmesan cheese.  I'm not a big mayo fan!  We ended with balsamic cherry tomatoes on slices of sourdough bread.  Those were also tasty!

I had the Frank Family Zinfandel.  Frank Family is one of my favorites.  Their Zin is easy on the stomach! They carry mostly local brands.  There's a lot of grape growers in Oakley, Brentwood and Lodi.  Rest decor

<review>Updating a year later and this place is still great post-covid. Nice food selection with wine and feel safe with friendly & professional staff.

old review:
I have dinner and appetizers quite a bit next store at Attraversiamo which is always good, but recently discovered the pleasure of going back and forth between the two.

I felt like a glass of wine last week and went over and received some great recommendations after describing the type of Cab I like with a great cheese plate. <Date>1595552757975</Date>< Rate>

< review>
It's tough to find a good sports bar in DTLA. In that regard xLanes is a bit of a hidden gem in Little Tokyo, Arts District adjacent. Lots of TVs. 3 big projector TVs are front & center. They play almost everything except boxing & UFC main events. Great place to catch Lakers, Dodgers & NFL games. Game audio is played. Add a food menu, a full bar, a fun bartending staff & it's going to be a good time. ‚öæüçªüèàüçªüèÄüçªüèí</review>

<review>Located inside Little Tokyo Galleria Market is x-lanes. A bowling alley, pool hall, full sports bar, latest state of the art arcade center, private karaoke rooms, and banquet rooms all in one place. They have something for everyone.

I've been here a few times for drinks and karaoke.There are plenty of up-to-date songs with fun neon lights, tables, and chairs. Karaoke on the weekend is  $50/an hr. A bit pricey IMO.

The bar area has several big screen TVs and almost always has it on a sports channel. There are plenty of tables and booths. Drink prices are relatively cheap.

I love the bowling area. There are spacious seating and table for each lane. You can even have your own private party at the table. They offer party packages that includes food & bowling. There's very loud music playing in this part of the venue.

All in all, it's a great place to come for some fun & games.< /review>< gmap_id>

<Gmap_id>0x80c2c639a6f4292d:0xff6517f71cd550c9</Gmap_id><Text>It has a nice variety of things to do.  There is a bar with TV's to watch sporting games.  Pool tables and  bowling, but the lanes are usually busy, I  was told you can call the day ahead and reserve your lane.  There is an arcade , but  many of the games were broke.  ID is required to get in even if you are not drinking so don't forget it at home.  The bar servers are friendly and fast. If you didn't want to eat at one of the local spots near by they  do have a restaurant, and you can order from the bar as well.   It is very outdated with it's look and kept environment. <Date>1478104745533< /Date><rate>3<//rate>< Text>
Great Bowling alley, clean lanes atmosphere is great too. Bit of a wait for a lane but good food and drink selection at the bar, and lots of arcade games while you wait. Only thing I would change is the hourly rate. It's pretty expensive. And with Kids they tend to Bowl slow. I prefer the old days when you paid per game, and didn't feel so rushed to cram in as many games as you can into one hour. Especially at $70 an hour for a weekend night. Think that's a bit greedy. But overall the experience was great. Just way too pricey for bowling, and they wouldn't let the kids parents watch the kids bowl cause only 6 people per lane. Even if your not Bowling you can't just sit and watch your kids Bowl. There policy doesn't make a lot of sense.</Text>

101491025563625720540< /user>
<Pics>None< /Pics>< review>
I hate bowling...
So bypass the endless aisles of lanes.

But I like drinking!
So please stop at the full service bar. Yes they have beers, wines, and spirits and reasonably priced. No it's not happy hour but its what's to be expected at a gaming lounge.

I hate dirty bathrooms.
So please don't use these bathrooms. They were filthy. The smell of vomit and feces quickly filled my nose upon entering. And the conditions of the stalls matched the order.

But I do like karaoke!
They have two options. 1. Rent a room per hour to sing your heart out (gets kinda of pricey. 2. Pay $5 to record yourself in a super cool booth to your favorite hits. I choose the later. Least you get to walk home with a CD you can possibly sell in a Superior parking lot. But either option leads to a super fun time.

Overall this is an awesome place for fun. In addition to what's mentioned above, they do have billiards, food (pretty tasty pizza!!) and validated parking. What more could you ask for!</review>

<Date>1462259342035< /Date><Rating>3<//Rating>< review>
This place in general looks new. Not run down or aging as other places.
The arcade was mediocre. They need to bring in more exciting and brand new games that people would actually get hooked to or bring classic arcade games.
The bowling lanes are well kept.
They have several karaoke rooms which are about $30/HR on a weekday. The sound system is okay. The songs are updated.
They have a dart game system that you pay the machine cash to. The billiard hall tables are also well kept.
They have a liquor bar.

It's located at the top floor of the building so it's a good place to go after having a buffet party next door at Manna.<//review>

< review>
Diversified fun for the whole: individual, couple, circle of friends, family, etc.  XLanes has something for everybody featuring 9 pool tables; full-bar; arcade; and of course bowling lanes.

Located on the 3rd floor of the Little Tokyo Plaza off Alameda, XLanes is a welcoming business to this otherwise empty plaza.

Prices are a bit on the steep side.  An hour of pool is $15, add a couple of beers (cheap) at $5 each and your one our of fun will end up costing you about $25.  That is a pretty expensive hour of fun.

I think other people were wiser than I to this as the bar was packed.  I think people decided to put all of their entertainment money on their bar tap than on pool or bowling.</review>

<Date>1442241299640<//Date><Rate>2</Rate>< Review>
I've had two experiences at XLanes, one being a four star, the other a one, so two stars is well deserved. A few months ago, I went there with a few coworkers during the week to have a few drinks and blew off some steam. A few beers later and a couple games of bowling, it was a great night. Good atmosphere and decent service.

Now a couple weeks ago, I again revisited XLanes, this time on a Saturday afternoon for some family fun time. The lane we were given was next to a kid's bday party, which was unnecessary with a dozen other lanes open. The adults at the party, we cannot call them parents since they were doing no parenting, proceeded to sit and chat while they're children through multiple bowling balls down their lanes, jamming the machine, and spilled into our lane, ruining one of my daughter's frames. I called for a worker and someone went and fixed their lane, but never did anyone from XLanes apologize nor do anything to correct this idiocy.

Unfortunately, it seems that XLanes has lost a customer.<//Review>

< text>
Seems like a lot of the bowling alleys are hard to come by around downtown Los Angeles.  This place is located in the Mitsuwa plaza, formerly known as Yohan in J-Town if you guys didn't know that.  This place reminds me of another bowling alley venue in Puente Hills called Round 1 with the combination of bowling, snookers and karaoke.  They also have a nice bar on the side for people who enjoy a couple of nightcaps or two.  The only thing are the prices for bowling it's pretty expensive so be prepared to spend lots of money.  Make sure to go with a bigger crowd to get some type of discount.<//text>
